No. 1574 of 18)</span><span style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:110%'>) </span><![endif]--><!-- [if supportFields]><spanstyle='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:110%'><span style='mso-element:field-end'></span></span><![endif]--><span style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%;">: <span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"> </span>None represented. </span></p><p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: center;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;">JUDGMENT</span></u></strong></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 22.5pt; line-height: 110%;"><strong><u><span style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-variant: small-caps;">Muhammad Imman Ali, J:</span></u></strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%;"> These petitions for leave to appeal have been filed against the judgement and order dated the 16<sup>th</sup> day of November, 2017 passed by the High Court Division in Company Matter Nos.120, 121 and 122 of 2017 dismissing the same. The connected contempt petitions were rejected. Since all the petitions relate to the same subject matter and arise out of one judgement of the High Court Division, they are dealt with by this single judgement.</span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">2.<span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">             </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">The facts relevant for disposal of these civil petitions for leave to appeal are as follows:</span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; line-height: 110%; tab-stops: 27.0pt; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">         </span>Respondent No.1-company in each matter is a family owned private company. The petitioner and respondent Nos.2 to 4 are full brothers, while respondent Nos.5 to 8 are their spouses respectively. These are the only shareholders of the respondent-companies. As per Articles of Association of the respondent-companies, the </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">petitioner </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">shall be the first Managing </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">Director </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of the </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">respondent-c</span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">ompanies and </span></span><span class="FontStyle26"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">shall continue in that office for a period of five </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">years and respondent No.2 shall be the first and permanent Chairman of the respondent-companies and they shall continue in their respective offices until they voluntarily resign or become </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">disqualified to </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">be </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">a Director of the respondent-companies. N</span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">o need has been felt for any change in the internal management of the respondent-companies, including the signatories of the bank accounts, or change in the office of Chairman or Managing Director. The bank accounts of the companies were to be operated upon signature of the Managing Director (the petitioner) and any one of the other Directors, as should be nominated by the Board. Accordingly, the bank accounts of the respondent-c</span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">ompanies </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">are being operated on the joint signatures of the petitioner and any one of respondent Nos.2 or 3. The </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">respondent-companies’ financial </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">success and </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">position </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">as </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">market </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">leader</span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">s</span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;"> have been the main reason for allowing the management to </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">continue </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">as </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">it is. </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">There has absolutely never been any complaint or allegation against the Managing Director (the petitioner) or about the management of the respondent-companies. It is mentioned further that out of the four Directors of the respondent-companies, the petitioner and respondent Nos.2 and 3 were the most active, while respondent No.4 was more dormant. In the meantime, the c</span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: SimHei; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">hildren of the shareholders of the respondent-</span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: SimHei; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">companies began attaining majority and </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: SimHei; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">returning to the country, </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">having received education in the leading Universities of the West. The shareholders of the respondent-companies therefore considered it fit to appoint their sons to various executive capacities in the Paradise Group in the hope and expectation of grooming them for smooth transition of the family business to the next generation. But as ill luck would have it, due to the high handed behaviour of the son of respondent No.2, the relationship of amity that had existed among the brothers previously has broken down, and disputes and differences have arisen between them with respect to the affairs of the respondent-companies. The hitherto congenial atmosphere in the respondent-companies and among the brothers/shareholders/directors has been so much vitiated and soured by his conduct that his uncles, namely, the petitioner and respondent No.3 were greatly hurt. In the background of the above facts and circumstances, respondent No.2 made some one sided proposals to resolve the dispute and differences, which the petitioner and respondent No.3 found to be lacking in good faith and as promoting the personal interests of respondent No.2 and his son, </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">undermining </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">stake </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of the </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">other brothers. </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">This </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">prompted </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the petitioner and respondent No.3 to </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">make </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">counter proposals to resolve the disputes and differences by effectively partitioning the businesses and undertakings of the Paradise Group as well as </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">immovable </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">properties </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">acquired </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">in their individual names, keeping the business interest of the respondent-companies uppermost. Unfortunately such proposals did not yield any solution. In the course of the dispute that has arisen between the shareholders/directors of the respondent-companies, the disputants have coalesced </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">into </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">by and large </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">two groups, with the petitioner </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">and</span></span> <span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">respondent No.3 being on one side and respondent Nos.2 and 4 being on the other. In the above situation, respondent No.2 at </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">the </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">instigation and incitement of his son, issued a notice dated 12.12.2016 convening a meeting of the Board of Directors of the respondent-companies at its office to be held on 22.12.2016, with the purported agenda for (i) discussing about the incompetency and financial irregularities committed by the Managing Director and to remove the petitioner from the post of Managing Director, (ii) appointing a new Managing Director, (iii) authorising signatories to operate bank accounts </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">of </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the company and authorising a person to make all kind of correspondences with the Bank and other financial institutions, and (iv) any other matter(s) with the permission </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">of </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the Chairman. </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">A</span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">instant Company Matter </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; The High Court Division vide order dated </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">13.04.2017, stayed agenda </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">Nos.1 and 2 of the said </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">notice </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">dated 09.04.2017 of the meeting of the Board of Directors to be held on 17.04.2017. The petitioner claimed that the Board </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">of </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">Directors has no authority to consider the issue </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">of </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">re-employment or the extension of the term of office of</span></span> <span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">Md. Mobarak </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">Hossain as Managing</span></span> <span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">Director </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of the company/this is a matter to be discussed </span></span><span class="FontStyle20"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">in the </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">General Meeting. The High Court Division held that 'agenda No.1 is sub-judice before the High Court Division, while agenda No.2 is not couched in a proper language and prima-facie makes an impression that the Board intends to take decision that is not within its competence as per section 110(3) of the Act. Therefore, the High Court Division did not pass any order of injunction on conducting General Meeting of the shareholders of the said companies. Rather, the High Court Division in clear term stated that as per section 110 only shareholders can consider the issue of reappointment or extension of tenure of </span></span><span class="FontStyle20"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">Managing Director. I</span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">n compliance </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">with the aforesaid order dated 13.03.2017 passed by the High Court Division another notice was issued on 15.04.2017 for Board Meeting of the said companies to be held on 19.04.2017 to call Extraordinary General Meeting to discuss about expiration of tenure of Mobarak Hossain as Managing Director of the company as per section 110 of the Companies Act and to consider the issue of re-appointment or the extension of the term of office of Mobarak Hossain as Managing Director. The meeting of the Board of Directors was held on 17.04.2017 and the petitioner Mobarak Hossain attended the said meeting as Managing Director. Members of the Board expressed their utter dissatisfaction since Mobarak Hossain is not signing necessary documents and papers for issuing PG, BG, L/C and other credit facilities. The Board under agenda No.4 adopted resolution requesting Mobarak Hossain to perform his duties and </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">responsibilities. The Board </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">Directors in its meeting, </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">held on 19.04.2017, also decided to call Extra General Meeting </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the company on 17.05.2017 to consider the issue </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">re-appointment, </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">employment, or extension </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of the term of office of the petitioner, Md. Mobarak Hossain, as Managing Director of the company. Thereafter, the </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">shareholders of respondent </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">No.1-</span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">company in </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">its Extraordinary General Meeting held on 17.05.2017 adopted special resolution deciding that the petitioner, Md. Mobarak Hossain will not be re-appointed, re-employed and his term </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of office as Managing Director of </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">company </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">will not be renewed, </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">since </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">his </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">tenure </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">as Managing </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">Director </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">has exceeded the statutory limit or 5(five) years and there were serious allegations of misconduct and misappropriation of company funds and assets of the company, hence, the shareholders of the said companies decided not to re-appoint the petitioner as Managing Director in their Extraordinary General<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>Meeting held on 17.05.2017. The </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">shareholders also adopted </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">another special resolution and have resolved to appoint Majibur Rahman </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">as </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">new Director instead of the petitioner in compliance with the Articles </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of A</span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">ssociation and </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">Companies Act </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">1994. The </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">petitioner </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">did not </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">challenge the legality </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of the special resolution adopted on 17.05.2017. There is no order of the Court staying operation of the special resolution dated 17.05.2017 adopted by the shareholders of company. The shareholders </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the said companies have the legal authority to adopt special resolution not to reappoint or extend tenure of the petitioner as Managing Director of the company. The said special resolution adopted on 17.05.2017 is clearly a valid resolution as two-third of </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">the shareholders of the said companies </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">were present </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">in </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">that </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">meeting </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">and the resolution was adopted unanimously. There is no substance in the claim of the petitioner, Mobarak Hossain, that the shareholders of respondent No.1-company adopted the said special resolution on 17.05.2017 in violation of the order of this Court dated 27.03.2017 and 13.03.2017. The High Court Division vide the said orders dated 27.03.2017 and 13.03.2017 did not prohibit the shareholders from adopting any resolution regarding re-appointment or extension of term of the petitioner as Managing Director whose tenure of office already had been expired. Rather, the High Court Division in clear terms stated that as per section 110 only the shareholders can consider the issue of re-appointment or extension of tenure of Managing Director.</span></span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">5.<span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">             </span></span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-fareast-font-family: SimHei; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">Respondent No.</span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: SimHei; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">2 by filing </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-fareast-font-family: SimHei; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">another </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: SimHei; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">affidavit-in-opposition on 05.11.2017 stated that respondent No.2 is the founder Chairman and Director of the respondent-companies since their inception/establishment in 1985. Paradise Group is the brain-child of respondent No.2. Respondent No.2 established M/S </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: SimHei; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">Paradise </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: SimHei; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">Electrics in 1976 and was involved in trading </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">of electrical goods.
