T</span></span><span class="FontStyle20"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">he heirs/successors of the </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">Managing </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">Director, the petitioner, have already registered the said </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">companies </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">at RJSC and started business of the company. Thus the petitioner along with his heirs/successors has established a competitive business in clear breach of the </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">Articles </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">Association, </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">and the </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">provisions </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">laid down in the MOA of the said companies. According to the provisions of Articles of Association, the petitioner cannot involve directly or indirectly in any business which is in competition with respondent No.1-company. It is provided that shares of the Director will be forfeited if he involves in any competitive business. It is evident that the petitioner, being the Managing Director, is involved in the competitive business by facilitating </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">his son </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">and daughter in </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">establishing </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">those companies. T</span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">he petitioner, </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">being Managing Director of </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the Paradise Group, </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">misused his power by deliberately utilising his heirs/successors and instructed them illegally to </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">form </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the said new company by using the name/word 'Paradise'. Further he instructed his son Moshiur Hossain Uday and daughter Mehbuba Hossain Upama to form the new company "Star Paradise" and accordingly as per his </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">instructions </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">after forming the said Company, they started production of cables, fiber optics, fan, pole and switch etc. which is clearly a competitive business and contrary to clause 12 </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">of </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the said MOA and against the provisions of the existing MOA of Paradise Group. The petitioner, being the </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">Managing </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">Director of respondent No.1-company, illegally supplied electricity connection to his son's company, "Star Paradise Limited" and "Fidelity Holdings Limited", from the existing connection of Paradise Spinning Mills Limited without taking prior approval from the Board of Directors and also without any permission from the Electricity Board of Bangladesh. This is a clear violation of the laws of this country and such violation would be considered a criminal offence in the eye of law. The petitioner being Managing Director of Companies Paradise Group was misusing his powers. The petitioner, instead of taking any steps against the said Star Paradise Limited, allowed his son to cause serious financial loss to the Paradise Cables Limited. As such, the petitioner is in clear breach and violation of the Articles of Association of Paradise Cables Limited and that the petitioner, being the Managing Director of companies of Paradise Group was involved in activities to sabotage the fame and glory of Paradise Group and also to gain illegal benefit </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">and advantage from </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">good</span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">will of the </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">name </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of the Group in the business community and market. Till date, the petitioner has not disclosed the accounts of Paradise Fashions Limited, Paradise Hi-Design Limited and never gave dividends to the shareholders and directors of the company. Then most surprisingly, it came to light that the petitioner most fraudulently fabricated and forged resolution dated 20.04.2016 to AB bank Limited, Motijheel Branch stating that they are </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">authorised </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">to renew the composite </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">credit </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">facilities which was due to expire on 30.06.2016 and make all correspondences with the bank singly and also to receive or execute any document(s) relating to the credit facilities. Moniar Hossain was abroad at the time of the meeting and respondent No.2 was not aware of such meeting. No notice was also served for such meeting. Hence, there was no quorum and the said meeting and the resolution has no validity in the eye of law. Therefore, the said resolution dated 20.04.2016 is forged, unlawful and void and the petitioner again </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">resorted </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">to illegal means to </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">further </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">his evil ploy of robbing the respondent company in broad daylight. In </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">a </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">similar </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">fraudulent manner, </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the petitioner fabricated and forged another resolution dated 04.11.2016 that they are </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">authorised </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">to make all correspondences with the bank singly and also to receive or execute any document(s) relating to a credit facility. Respondent No.2, respondent No.3 and Moniar Hossain were not present at the meeting and hence there was no quorum. Further, the resolution stated that the </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">meeting </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">took place at "4 a.m." which also substantiates that the same is forged as </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">a </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">business meeting cannot </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">take place </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">outside of business hours. Therefore, the said resolution dated 20.04.2016 is forged, unlawful and void and the petitioner </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">again resorted to illegal means to further their evil ploy. The </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">incompetency of the petitioner to act as Managing Director of the </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">respondent-company is also evident from </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the fact that the petitioner issued </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">office </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">order </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">on </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">07.01.2017 declaring holiday for all officers who are working in the Head Office of the respondent company contrary to the declared holiday circular/leave circular, 2017 of the company. The petitioner most illegally declared that holiday so that the meeting of Board of Directors could not be held on 08.01.2016. This proves that the petitioner is totally unfit to perform his responsibilities. The petitioner is carrying out his responsibilities whimsically and arbitrarily which is seriously prejudicial to the interest of the company.</span></span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">6.<span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">             </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">The petitioner has filed, on 12.11.2017, an affidavit-in-opposition against the 2nd affidavit-in-opposition filed by respondent No.2 on 06.11.2017, in which the petitioner has denied some facts and has stated some facts to be matters of record. However, the petitioner has admitted to have received the notice dated 15.04.2017, whereby a Board meeting was <span style="letter-spacing: -.3pt;">called on 19.04.2017 to decide about summoning</span> an EGM for the purpose of taking </span></span><span class="FontStyle22"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">decision as per section 110(3) of </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the Act. </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">As regards, the fact of holding that Board meeting on 19.04.2017 and the EGM resolution adopted on 17.05.2017, the petitioner stated that these are matters of record.</span></span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">7.<span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">             </span></span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">Upon hearing the parties and considering the evidence and materials on record, the High Court Division by the judgement and order dated 16.11.2017 dismissed the petitions. Then the petitioner preferred the civil petitions for leave to appeal before this </span></span><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">Division</span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span></span></span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">8.<span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">             </span></span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">Mr. Rokanuddin Mahmud, learned Senior Advocate, appearing on behalf of the petitioner submitted </span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">that the High Court Division erred in law and upon the facts in failing to appreciate that respondent No.1-company was a family owned-company in the nature of a quasi-partnership in which the petitioner, along with his brothers, had an equal stake and a legitimate expectation to participate in </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">management, </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">and that the other shareholders were acting in a manner so as to exclude him from such management, which entitled him to relief under section 233 of the Companies Act, 1994. He submitted that the High Court Division made a plainly erroneous finding of fact to the effect that the petitioner did not challenge the resolution dated </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">17.05.2017 by way </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">amendment </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">to the main petition or in the prayer portion of the main petition, and that the interlocutory application of the petitioner dated 06.06.2017 filed in matter No.120 of 2017 praying for stay of the resolution dated 17.05.2017 was not pressed at any stage of hearing, whereas the petitioner has categorically challenged the EGM dated 17.05.2017 in his affidavit-in-reply dated 12.11.2017 and his application dated 06.06.2017 which was pressed at the time of final hearing, and that in the context of an application under </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">section </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">233 of the Companies Act, 1994, the Court is not confined to granting relief in the terms prayed for in the application, but may particularly upon consideration that the cause of action in such cases are typically a continuing one, grant any other appropriate relief. He submitted that the High Court Division erred in law and upon the facts in rejecting the petitioner's contention that the EGM dated 17.05.2017 was invalid as no notice was served upon the petitioner inasmuch that such decision of the High Court Division is based upon a plainly erroneous finding of fact, that the petitioner was served with the material notices of convening of the EGM dated 17.05.2017 through courier, whereas the </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">addresses </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">used </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">for </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">courier </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">are incorrect as there is nothing on record to show that the notice was effectively served upon the petitioner, and hence the High Court Division ought to have found that the EGM dated 17.05.2017 was invalid for not having served the notice upon the petitioner. He submitted that the High Court Division erred in law and upon the facts inasmuch that it proceeded purely on the basis of conjecture and surmise in observing that the petitioner's prayer to buy him out is not considered as just and proper one considering that he had the upper hand in controlling and conducting the affairs of the companies and completely failed to appreciate that the petitioner's interests being a minority is being highly prejudiced by the actions of respondent Nos.2 to 4 as evident from the fact that respondent Nos.2 to 4 having already amended the Articles of Association, and their enabling of respondent No.2's misappropriation of the company's income in his personal </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">account and thereby depriving the petitioner from his legitimate share in the capital and profit of the company. He</span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;"> submitted</span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;"> that </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the High Court Division erred in law and upon the facts </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">inasmuch as</span></span> <span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">it proceeded </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">purely on the basis of conjecture and surmise in arriving at the conclusion that the petitioner breached his fiduciary duty and completely failing to appreciate the fact that the petitioner was in fact trying to save the company from the misappropriations taking place under the influence of respondent No.2 by way of collection of company fund in his personal account. He submitted </span></span><span class="FontStyle28"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">that the </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">High Court Division erred in law and upon the facts inasmuch as it proceeded purely on the basis of conjecture and </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">surmise in arriving at the conclusion </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">that the petitioner used his </span></span><span class="FontStyle35"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">position or Managing Director and his network as well as the brand name </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">and </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">goodwill of "Paradise Group" in sponsoring and nourishment of "Star Paradise" established in the name of </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">his </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">son and thus the High Court Division having completely failed to appreciate that "Star Paradise" is not involved in any business directly or indirectly competing with any of the concerns of Paradise Group inasmuch as Star Paradise is only involved in the business of electric fan, switch and socket which is not the business of any of the companies of Paradise Group. He lastly submitted that the High Court Division erred in law and upon the facts in delivering the erroneous observation, that "quorum" is not or cannot be a pre-requisite to call and hold a meeting and that if any general meeting or a Board meeting cannot be called to order for lack of quorum, then the meeting comes into existence, though it cannot transact the business for want of quorum.</span></span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 105%; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 105%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">9.<span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">             </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 105%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">Mr. A.F. Hasan Ariff, learned Senior Advocate appeared on behalf of respondent No.3 in Civil Petition for Leave to Appeal Nos.1572, 1573 and 1574 of 2018, Mr. Ajmalul Hossain, learned Senior Advocate appeared on behalf of respondent No.2 in Civil Petition for Leave to Appeal Nos.1572, 1573 and 1574 of 2018 and Mr. Sheik Fazle-Noor Taposh, learned Advocate appeared on behalf of respondent No.4 in Civil Petition for Leave to Appeal Nos.1573 and 1574 of 2018. They made submissions in support of the impugned judgement and order of the High Court Division. </span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">10.<span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">         </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">We have considered the submissions of the learned Advocates for the parties concerned, perused the impugned judgement and order of the High Court Division and other connected papers on record.</span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">11.<span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">      </span></span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">From the findings of the High Court Division, it appears that </span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">all </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">the petitions had been filed before the Company Bench under section 233 of the Act challenging the Board resolutions dated 16.02.2017 and 23.02.2017, whereby the directorship of the petitioner was recorded to have fallen vacant with reference to the provisions of section 108</span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">(l</span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">)(f) of the Act, for non-attendance of three consecutive meetings of the Board of Directors without leave of absence. The question that has been raised, for decision of the High Court Division, is whether the said Board meetings, none of which could be called to order for lack of quorum, could be treated as </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">"Board meetings'" </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">for the purpose of treating the petitioner as an </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">"absentee", </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">in those meetings in view of the provisions of section 108(1)(f) of the Act. In other words, whether </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">'absence' </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">of the petitioner in those Board meetings, that could not be called to order for want of quorum, could be treated as </span></span><span class="FontStyle24"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">'absence' </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">to </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">attract </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">the mischief of section 108(l)(f) of the Act. However, the operation of the said Board resolutions dated 16.02.2017 (referred in a letter dated 23.02.2017) was stayed by the Company Bench, by an order dated 27.03.2017 at the time of admission of the petition, and the petitioner was continuing as the </span></span><span class="FontStyle25"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Cambria; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">Managing </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">Director and he was also receiving all notices of the Board meetings. </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">Subsequently, </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">the </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">respondent-</span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">companies called another Board meeting, by a notice dated 09.04.2017, scheduled to be held on 17.04.2017, but the petitioner filed an application for injunction on 12.04.2017, against that notice dated 09.04.2017. There were as many as 8 agendas in the said notice. The Company Bench, by another order dated 13.04.2017, had restrained the respondents from transacting agenda Nos.1 and 2 and the </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">respondents </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">have obeyed the said orders. In passing the order of restraint against agenda No.1, the Court's view was that, agenda No.1 was sub-judice, while agenda No.2, purporting to take a decision with regard to the tenure of the petitioner as Managing Director vis-à-vis section 110(3) should be taken up in a general meeting, i.e. not in the Board meeting dated 17.04.2017.</span></span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">12.<span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">      </span></span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">It appears from the materials on record that, in view of </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">the<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">   </span>order<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">   </span></span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">dated<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">   </span></span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">13.04.2017 </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">and since the issue of the tenure/reappointment of the petitioner (MD) is to be decided in a general meeting, the companies have, thereafter, by a notice dated 15.04.2017, called a Board meeting on 19.04.2017, to discuss about summoning an EGM for taking decision about the issue of extension of the term of office of the petitioner as the Managing </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">Director and/or </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">his </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">re-appointment, </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">as per section 110(3) of the Act and other related issues. The petitioner has received the said notice as acknowledged, vide his letter dated 18.04.2017, but he did not attend the Board meeting dated 19.04.2017. However, that Board meeting was held on 19.04.2017 and it further appears from the Board resolution dated 19.04.2017, that the Board of Directors had called an Extraordinary General Meeting (EGM) on 17.05.2017 and notices of the EGM were served upon the all shareholders, including the petitioner. The petitioner received the notices of the EGM, vide Annexure- Y (20) series. The said EGM was held on 17.05.2017, in</span></span> <span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">which 6 </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">shareholders, </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">out </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">8 shareholders, were present. The required number of quorum being present, the members (shareholders) present in the meeting took up the agenda regarding the tenure of the office of the petitioner, in view of the provisions of section 110(3) of the Act.</span></span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 109%; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">13.<span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">      </span></span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">The High Court Division found that, as against agenda </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">No.1, </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">it has </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">been recorded in the </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">minutes </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">the said EGM dated 17.05.2017 that, </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">"Md. Maniar Hossain, director of the company informed the meeting that the tenure of Managing Director has already expired. As per section 110 of the Companies Act, 1994, maximum duration of a Managing Director is 05(five) years. Thereafter, the Managing Director is required to be re-appointed by the shareholders. But Md. Mobarak Hossain has not been re-appointed by the shareholders in compliance with Companies Act. As such, the tenure of the Managing Director has come to an end by operation of law. The shareholders must now reappoint him to continue as Managing Director or appoint a new Managing Director. Mr. Md. Maniar Hossain informed the shareholders that since 2015, the company has gone into a deadlock and has been suffering from business losses. The existing Managing Director, Mr. Md. Mobarak Hossain, lost confidence of the other three Directors and for last 06(six) months he is not performing his duties and responsibilities by failing to execute necessary documents relating to PG, BG, L/C and other credit facilities. He is not even signing cheques for which company fails to make payment of salary to the staff. There is also serious allegation of misappropriation, mismanagement against him. He is also acting against interest of the company by establishing competitive company named Star Paradise Limited and Fidelity Holdings Limited by usurping and exploiting resources of the company. In these circumstances, to protect interest of the company and shareholders Mr. Md. Maniar Hossain urged shareholders not to renew tenure of Mr. Md. Mobarak Hossain as Managing Director anymore. Honourable Vice-Chairman of the company Md. Majibar Rahman agreed with Mr. Md. Maniar Hossain and claimed that although the Managing Director Md. Mobarak Hossain has been the Managing Director of the company since its inception and managed to make the company a profitable concern, however, his conduct since 2015 is destroying the brand image of the company and he is failing to perform his </span></em></span><span class="FontStyle24"><em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">duties as Managing Director in the best interest </span></em></span><span class="FontStyle18"><em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of the shareholders and the company. Even, he has sent several letters to the Bank stating that he is no more interested to give Bank Guarantee and also requested the bank not to allow the company credit facilities. There are allegations of impropriety and misconduct against him from various quarters. In view of the existing unfortunate situation, the honourable Vice-Chairman strongly urged the shareholders not to renew tenure of Mr. Md. Mobarak Hossain as Managing Director of the company in order to protect interest of the </span></em></span><span class="FontStyle24"><em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">shareholders and the company. </span></em></span><span class="FontStyle18"><em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">He also agreed that Mr. Md. Mobarak Hossain </span></em></span><span class="FontStyle24"><em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Courier New'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">may </span></em></span><span class="FontStyle18"><em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">continue to serve as Director of the company.”</span></em></span> <span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; Hence, upon the disposal </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">of </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 109%; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">the main petition, this application has become infructuous. </span></span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; His term as Managing Director was not extended nor was he re-appointed in the Extraordinary General Meeting dated 17.05.2017. mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">as</span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; Besides, the allegations of creating </span></span><span class="FontStyle33"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal;">two forged resolutions </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">dated 20.04.2016 and 04.11.2016 sent to the banker of these companies tantamount to extreme breach of fiduciary duties by the petitioner. He even did not pay any heed to the request made to him by other directors in the Board meeting dated 17.04.2017 to sign necessary documents and papers for issuing PG, BG and L/C and other credit facilities all of which were indispensable to run the respondent companies as going concern. Hence, the allegation that the </span></span><span class="FontStyle25"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-bidi-font-family: Cambria; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; text-indent: 0in; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">17.<span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">      </span></span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">It appears from the record that in the instant case, though the petitioner is a minority shareholder, he however, had the upper hand in controlling and conducting the affairs of the companies, for more than 5(five) years. Hence, he cannot be said to have been oppressed since he was at the helm of affairs of the companies. Therefore, his prayer to buy him out is not considered as just and proper one.</span></span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">18.<span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">      </span></span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">For any meeting to conduct business, quorum is necessary. Whether or not quorum exists can only be ascertained when the meeting is about to commence. Hence, lack of quorum does not negative the existence of the meeting, but means only that no business could be transacted due to lack of quorum. Consequently absence in such a meeting is certainly absence as understood in section 108 of the Act. </span></span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">19.<span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">         </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span class="FontStyle30"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">We are of the view that the High Court Division correctly held that </span></span><span class="FontStyle29"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">the Board </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">meetings which could not be called to order due to lack </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; mso-fareast-font-family: MingLiU; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Bookman Old Style'; letter-spacing: -.2pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">of quorum were 'meetings' in the eye of law and </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;">the petitioner's </span></span><span class="FontStyle18"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;">deliberate </span></span><span class="FontStyle17"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;">absence without leave must be treated as 'absence' in those meetings and will attract the mischief of section 108(1)(f) of the Act and his office would fall vacant by operation of law, for which no resolution need be taken, save to record the fact of vacation of the office of the absentee in the minutes and to submit a Form XII to the RJSC and, thereafter, that director will not be entitled to receive any notice of Board meeting or to attend the meeting of the Board. The High Court Division further held that </span></span><span class="FontStyle31"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11pt;">although the impugned Board resolution dated 16.02.2017 has become infructuous because of the order of stay and the subsequent </span></span><span class="FontStyle32"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11pt;">EGM decision </span></span><span class="FontStyle31"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11pt;">dated 17.05.2017, however, the conduct of the petitioner in deliberately absenting himself from three consecutive Board meetings, so that quorum could not be formed and the meetings could not be called to order, amounts to absence without leave in the said Board meetings, within the meaning and for the purpose of section 108 (1)(f) of the Act and the </span></span><span class="FontStyle32"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11pt;">impugned Board resolution dated </span></span><span class="FontStyle31"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11pt;">16.02.2017 </span></span><span class="FontStyle32"><em><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11pt;">was </span></em></span><span class="FontStyle31"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11pt;">valid. Such conduct of the petitioner also amounts to breach of his statutory duties and it was clearly prejudicial to the interest of the company inasmuch as a director, by resorting to any tactics or measures whatsoever, cannot lead the company to a situation in which it will become impracticable for the company to call or hold its Board meeting or any other meetings permitted or required by law.</span></span></p><p class="MsoTitle" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; mso-outline-level: body-text; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><span class="FontStyle31"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11pt;">20.<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">         </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span class="FontStyle31"><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-size: 11pt;">In the facts and circumstances discussed above, we do not find any illegality or infirmity in the impugned judgement and order of the High Court Division.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 0in 27.0pt list .5in; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><!-- [if !supportLists]--><strong><span style="font-size: 11pt;">21.<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-weight: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">         </span></span></strong><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN;">Accordingly, the civil petitions for leave to appeal are dismissed.</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 110%; tab-stops: 31.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-bidi-font-family: Times-Roman;">           Ed. </span></strong></p><div style="mso-element: footnote-list;"><!-- [if !supportFootnotes]--><br clear="all"/><hr align="left" size="1" width="33%"/><!--[endif]--><div id="ftn1" style="mso-element: footnote;"><p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: none; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><a href="file:///H:/article/Issue__March__19(1)/Issue__March_19__C.%20P.%201572-1574%20of%2018__Muhammad%20Imman%20Ali,%20J___AD___3.doc#_ftnref1" name="_ftn1" style="mso-footnote-id: ftn1;" title=""><strong><u><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;">CIVIL PETITION FOR LEAVE TO APPEAL No</span></u></strong></a><strong><u><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;">s. 1572-1574 OF 2018 </span></u></strong></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-size: 9.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">(From the judgement and order dated the 16<sup>th</sup> day of November, 2017 passed by the High Court Division in Company Matter Nos.120, 121 and 122 of 2017 with corresponding Contempt Petition Nos.8, 10 and 9 of 2017 respectively).<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span></span></p></div></div></div></div>
747	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">Mrs. Sanjida Sarmin Vs.  Kazi Zahid Hossain and others, (Md. Nuruzzaman, J.) </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p><b>Case No:</b> Civil Revision No. 1648 of 2015 </p><p><b>Judge:</b>  Md. Nuruzzaman, J And S.H. Md. Nurul Huda Jaigirdar, J </p><p><b>Court:</b> High Court Division,</p><p><b>Advocate:</b> Mrs. Shahida Khatoon, Advocate with Mr. A. S. M. M. Kabir Khan, Advocate ,</p><p><b>Citation:</b>  2019(1) LNJ</p><p><b>Case Year:</b>  2018</p><p><b>Appellant:</b>  Mrs. Sanjida Sarmin </p><p><b>Respondent:</b>  Kazi Zahid Hossain and another  </p><p><b>Subject:</b>  Artha Rin Adalat Ain </p><p><b>Delivery Date:</b>  2019-11-27</p><!DOCTYPE html><div style="mso-element: footnote-list;"><div id="ftn1" style="mso-element: footnote;"><p class="MsoNormal"> </p></div></div><p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center;"><strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt;">HIGH COURT DIVISION </span></strong></p><p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center; line-height: 150%;"><strong><span style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; letter-spacing: -.3pt;">(CIVIL REVISIONAL JURISDICTION)</span></strong></p><table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="MsoNormalTable" style="margin-left: 5.4pt; border-collapse: collapse; mso-yfti-tbllook: 480; mso-padding-alt: 0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;"><tbody><tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 0; mso-yfti-firstrow: yes; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes;"><td style="width: 106.0pt; padding: 0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;" valign="top" width="141"><p class="MsoHeading8" style="margin: 0in -1.4pt 6.0pt 0in;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 11.0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman Bold',serif; letter-spacing: -.3pt; font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;">Md. padding: 0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;" width="21"><p align="center" class="MsoBodyTextIndent" style="text-align: center; line-height: 150%; margin: 0in -1.1pt 6.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;
